<tr>

</th>
<td>12 preludes
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1909-10
</td></tr>

</th>

<span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_mixed_chorus%2C_orchestra_%28arr%29&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For mixed chorus, orchestra (arr)</a></span>;
